                       <div data-reactid="462">
                        <div data-reactid="463">
                         People love this property because is the best location and most delightful room in Whittier!!! The private room is on the first floor of an historic home built by the Briggs Family in 1901. Sleep in the comfort of an antique four-poster King-size bed with cozy linens and your own private toilet. We are in the nicest area of Uptown Whittier near Hadley St. on Bright Ave. Walk to dozens of cafe's, restaurants, bakeries, shops, theatre, museum, &amp; Whittier College. A perfect room for a travel nurse.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="464">
                         We made some recent changes in this listing to provide a more reasonable price for one or two travelers. The adjoining living room (Fairy Garden Room) is now only available by special request for an additional cost of $20 per person per day for up to two additional people (max is four people). The room has a king bed but we can fit an air bed on the floor in the room to accommodate up to three adults. Special rate for travel nurses: $42 per night for stays over 30 days. This includes the monthly cleaning fee. Please message me to get the special offer. The Briggs' King Suite is on the first floor of an elegant vintage modern Victorian home built in 1901. The space is shared with Grandmother Turtles' House, an historic home and mind, body, spirit healing facility in Uptown Whittier, CA. The Briggs' King Suite has a super comfortable four-poster King bed with designer bedding, piles of pillows, and an atmosphere of joyous relaxation. The room also has a private toilet and sink, which is rare in historic homes like this. We don't have a television but guests have access to FiOS Wifi so bring your own device. Spa Room and shower - The shower room is an old-fashioned "wet bathroom" that was remodeled in 2014 with pebble flooring and designer wood wall tiles from the floor to the 10-foot ceiling. Guests love the spa atmosphere, scrumptious soaps, and other spa essentials. The spa room is shared with other guests. Kitchenette - cozy but fully stocked with all the elements needed to prepare gourmet meals. Guests are welcome to use the tea kettle, skillet, wok, toaster oven, microwave, and use the dishes, utensils, and glassware but please clean up after yourself and do not leave dirty dishes anywhere. The kitchenette is shared with other guests. We are bicycle friendly but please leave your furry friends at home. A little history about the property: Grandmother Turtles' House is a product of divine intervention. The physical structure was built by one of the founding fathers of Whittier in 1901 when he and his family settled in the suburbs of downtown Los Angeles. The historic home was so badly damaged in the 1987 Whittier Narrows Earthquake that the owners sold it for $1 to anyone who wanted to save the house. To do so, they had to pick it up and move it! A counseling center purchased the property, moved it three lots away onto the current location, and rebuilt the structure to meet modern requirements. It was further updated in 2004 when a prominent local lawyer purchased the property. In late 2014, our family acquired it to create something. We were not sure exactly what or why we were so moved to buy this beautiful old house, but the drive was so deep and strong it could not be ignored. We named the property “Grandmother Turtles' House" to reflect the concept that the weight of the world is on Grandmother Turtle's back. The property is a place where people help other people. We are now a group of holistic practitioners, healers, and teachers on the journey to assist humanity to find purpose and love for themselves and others. Vacancies are rare for both of our guest rooms because of our location and wonderful accommodations. If you see availability, then we highly recommend to reserve the room or send me a message if you have questions.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="465">
                         Nestled against the Puente Hills Wildlife Preserve, historic Uptown Whittier Village is the heart of a charming thriving city filled with art, music, spirituality, exquisite cuisine, and culture. Our property is steps away from Greenleaf Avenue, Whittier College, the Community Center, Whittier History Museum, and the beautiful Puente Hills Preserve. We are centrally located between Disneyland and Universal Studios and about 30 minutes to the mountains, or to the beach, Los Angeles Staples Center, LA Fashion District, LA Convention Center, Seal Beach, etc., etc., etc…. Uptown Whittier is a wonderful busy place! The Uptown Whittier Organization has a handy compilation of restaurants, businesses, events, and other wonderful places to go and things to do in Uptown. Visit the Uptown Whittier Association website for more information.
                        </div>

                         Our newly-renovated back house is centrally located to everything LA has to offer and still feels like a quiet retreat! It's the perfect private getaway to unwind after a long day of sight seeing or work. Great ambiance, a private outdoor patio, high ceilings, beautiful light, and a comfy bed. Good for couples or a family of three, solo adventurers, and business travelers.

                        <div data-reactid="1025">
                         Our studio is recessed in the back of our newly landscaped, lush backyard. It feels incredibly private, quiet and removed. It is newly-renovated, with vaulted wood ceilings, exposed beams, and mid-century furnishings. All the windows were refurbished in the original style of the turn of the century structure with sash weights. We have a wardrobe that is also turn of the century, adorned with original brass plates marking the right place for hosiery! We have a private brick patio out back with a four person table for dining and edison bulb string lights.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1026">
                         Harvard Heights is a historical neighborhood - the first suburb of downtown LA. It is filled with beautiful craftsman homes (including our own) from the turn of the century. That said, this neighborhood is definitely not Beverly Hills. It is culturally, racially, and economically diverse. It is a neighborhood in transition. So while our street and our home feel like a tranquil escape from the city, the main arteries around us do not! That said, they will take you to all parts of the city very quickly - Downtown, Culver City, Hollywood, even the beach are very easy to get to because of our proximity to major roads and highways.

                        <div data-reactid="1544">
                         Historic neighborhood and vintage building of classic Andalusian architecture. Antique elevator, exposed brick walls, fully equipped kitchen, danish mid century furniture and original hardwoods throughout. The second bed is a quality fold down couch. One the most centrally located neighborhoods in Los Angeles. Just a 20 minute drive to the canyon, beach, and hills. Hollywood, Echo Park, and Silver Lake are less than two miles north, and downtown is two miles southeast.

                        <div data-reactid="1677">
                         Authentic Mid Century decor with colorful modern flair. Our 1969 home has retro art &amp; furnishings. Easy 110/405 freeway access to all parts of Los Angeles &amp; Orange County. Relax in our master bedroom w/private bath &amp; balcony with cool ocean breezes.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1678">
                         Welcome to the best hidden Mid-Century Modern gem in Los Angeles! We nicknamed our home "The Dream Chasers' Retreat" for the guests we meet who visit and move to Los Angeles pursuing a dream. This city is full of amazing, creative visitors and locals who dream big. We are offering a modern, calming master bedroom with an amazing 260 degree view around the South Bay from the private balcony. The bright private en-suite bathroom has a lovely walk in shower. The bed is a comfortable queen size bed. This room is the master bedroom in The Dream Chaser's Retreat.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1679">
                         Our lovely home is in Harbor City, the southern most part of Los Angeles. This is 1 block east of Torrance and 2 miles from Redondo Beach. It is a safe, tranquil and quiet neighborhood. Most residents enjoy walking their dogs and getting outside to exercise daily. This neighborhood was built in 1969, when Mid-Century Modern met 1970s Retro designs. Within a 15-20 minute drive is Redondo Beach, Torrance Beach, San Pedro and Downtown Long Beach. Popular local destinations nearby are: - Redondo Beach Pier seafood bars &amp; restaurants, plus stunning sunsets - Torrance Beach bike path - Palos Verdes' cliff hiking to tide pools - Long Beach's Convention Center - San Pedro Cruise Warf &amp; Ports-O-Call - Old Town Torrance charm When eating out, our home is convenient to many different types of food: - Korean markets, BBQ &amp; Tofu House - Hawaiian restaurants - Japanese markets, bakeries, Ramen &amp; Sushi - Traditional American breakfast cafes - Asian Fusion restaurants (eg: Peruvian-Japanese, Chinese-Peruvian, Korean-Chinese) Across the street, Mulligans Family Fun is a great place for mini-golf/arcades. It's a one-of-a-kind experience staying at our colorful home.

                        <div data-reactid="2287">
                         From our illusionary floating bed to clean simple glass encased shower, the living space is cozy and spacious at same time. Kitchen inside is a simple setup (kitchenette) and out in the patio has access to bar-b-q set up to serve many if the guest(s) has a need to entertain. There are two bikes available on site and with Larchmount Village about ten minutes on bike, and for those that want LA mountain biking experience ask the hostess for the best spots. we are on the border of Korea town and Hancock park, minutes walk to Wilshire blvd. Since we are only ten minute walk to subway (bus is even closer), rail ,metro or whatever else you call it, guests can access Wilton theatre , Lacma , kodak theater, universal city studio and walk, historical downtown LA, long beach , LAX , la union station... (well. you get the point, anywhere!). And being in the heart of Korea-town, one has to adventure out to at least one of more then a dozen (walking distant) korean restaurants that we are surrounded by. But, at same time every type of ethnic food can be found close by and really good ones too! Stay with us as our guesthouse can definitely give the guest(s) a local flavor experience for those who seek it. For guest who wish to bring their dog, please see HOUSE RULE before asking for permission to bring their dog. We have a very strict requirements on the guest understanding that they must clean up after their dog and any damage their dog cause will be responsibility of the Guest. no Exception!!!!
